instruction is not counted.

## Object stats

<details>

managed dicts.

other names.

<th align="left"></th>
<th align="right">Count</th>

<tr>
<td align="left">
Optimization attempts
<details>
<summary></summary>

The number of times a potential trace is identified.  Specifically, this occurs in the JUMP BACKWARD instruction when the counter reaches a threshold.
</details>
</td>
<td align="right">0</td>
<td align="right"></td>
</tr>

<td align="left">
Traces created
<details>

</details>
</td>
<td align="right">0</td>
<td align="right"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Trace stack overflow
<details>
<summary></summary>

A trace is truncated because it would require more than 5 stack frames.
</details>
</td>
<td align="right">0</td>
<td align="right"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Trace stack underflow
<details>
<summary></summary>

A potential trace is abandoned because it pops more frames than it pushes.
</details>
</td>
<td align="right">0</td>
<td align="right"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Trace too long
<details>

</td>

<td align="right"></td>
</tr>
